\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
A\+V\+Options provide a generic system to declare options on arbitrary structs (\char`\"{}objects\char`\"{}). An option can have a help text, a type and a range of possible values. Options may then be enumerated, read and written to.\hypertarget{group__avoptions_avoptions_implement}{}\doxysubsection{Implementing A\+V\+Options}\label{group__avoptions_avoptions_implement}
This section describes how to add A\+V\+Options capabilities to a struct.

All A\+V\+Options-\/related information is stored in an \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_a_v_class}{A\+V\+Class}}. Therefore the first member of the struct should be a pointer to an \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_a_v_class}{A\+V\+Class}} describing it. The option field of the \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_a_v_class}{A\+V\+Class}} must be set to a N\+U\+L\+L-\/terminated static array of A\+V\+Options. Each \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_a_v_option}{A\+V\+Option}} must have a non-\/empty name, a type, a default value and for number-\/type A\+V\+Options also a range of allowed values. It must also declare an offset in bytes from the start of the struct, where the field associated with this \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_a_v_option}{A\+V\+Option}} is located. Other fields in the \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_a_v_option}{A\+V\+Option}} struct should also be set when applicable, but are not required.

The following example illustrates an A\+V\+Options-\/enabled struct\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keyword}{typedef} \textcolor{keyword}{struct }\mbox{\hyperlink{tests_2audio__fifo_8c_aa256d1a4aaeefeff416725ce6bd7d565}{test\_struct}} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{    \textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_a_v_class}{AVClass}} *\textcolor{keyword}{class};}
\DoxyCodeLine{    \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}      int\_opt;}
\DoxyCodeLine{    \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}    *str\_opt;}
\DoxyCodeLine{    \mbox{\hyperlink{audio__convert_8c_ae1affc9ca37cfb624959c866a73f83c2}{uint8\_t}} *bin\_opt;}
\DoxyCodeLine{    \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}      bin\_len;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\} \mbox{\hyperlink{tests_2audio__fifo_8c_aa256d1a4aaeefeff416725ce6bd7d565}{test\_struct}};}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_a_v_option}{AVOption}} \mbox{\hyperlink{tests_2opt_8c_a15da41cbdcc98199f1302576e15b56d3}{test\_options}}[] = \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \{ \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}test\_int"{}}, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}This is a test option of int type."{}}, offsetof(\mbox{\hyperlink{tests_2audio__fifo_8c_aa256d1a4aaeefeff416725ce6bd7d565}{test\_struct}}, int\_opt),}
\DoxyCodeLine{    \mbox{\hyperlink{group__avoptions_ggabd75aa30eb8ad6387672df9a1fa79444ac068b8f6afeeb293a13aeabb5d702411}{AV\_OPT\_TYPE\_INT}}, \{ .i64 = -\/1 \}, INT\_MIN, INT\_MAX \},}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \{ \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}test\_str"{}}, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}This is a test option of string type."{}}, offsetof(\mbox{\hyperlink{tests_2audio__fifo_8c_aa256d1a4aaeefeff416725ce6bd7d565}{test\_struct}}, str\_opt),}
\DoxyCodeLine{    \mbox{\hyperlink{group__avoptions_ggabd75aa30eb8ad6387672df9a1fa79444afadddce95ad3b690dd38644b458b96c4}{AV\_OPT\_TYPE\_STRING}} \},}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \{ \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}test\_bin"{}}, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}This is a test option of binary type."{}}, offsetof(\mbox{\hyperlink{tests_2audio__fifo_8c_aa256d1a4aaeefeff416725ce6bd7d565}{test\_struct}}, bin\_opt),}
\DoxyCodeLine{    \mbox{\hyperlink{group__avoptions_ggabd75aa30eb8ad6387672df9a1fa79444a2689966edbe494482dfdfaa4efdf95d3}{AV\_OPT\_TYPE\_BINARY}} \},}
\DoxyCodeLine{  \{ \mbox{\hyperlink{coverity_8c_a070d2ce7b6bb7e5c05602aa8c308d0c4}{NULL}} \},}
\DoxyCodeLine{\};}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_a_v_class}{AVClass}} \mbox{\hyperlink{tests_2opt_8c_a572a72bec21a00c1c0f9793f1fb7f6b1}{test\_class}} = \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{    .\mbox{\hyperlink{struct_a_v_class_aa8883e113a3f2965abd008f7667db7eb}{class\_name}} = \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}test class"{}},}
\DoxyCodeLine{    .item\_name  = \mbox{\hyperlink{group__lavu__log_ga791fcd0dba1d19fe0c3677509344328e}{av\_default\_item\_name}},}
\DoxyCodeLine{    .option     = \mbox{\hyperlink{tests_2opt_8c_a15da41cbdcc98199f1302576e15b56d3}{test\_options}},}
\DoxyCodeLine{    .version    = \mbox{\hyperlink{group__lavu__ver_ga36e17e3fc9bcbe5c55820a8ac8b47e3c}{LIBAVUTIL\_VERSION\_INT}},}
\DoxyCodeLine{\};}
\end{DoxyCode}


Next, when allocating your struct, you must ensure that the \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_a_v_class}{A\+V\+Class}} pointer is set to the correct value. Then, \mbox{\hyperlink{group__avoptions_gad4ca968e9058b39b2da630ad0a091bdb}{av\+\_\+opt\+\_\+set\+\_\+defaults()}} can be called to initialize defaults. After that the struct is ready to be used with the A\+V\+Options A\+PI.

When cleaning up, you may use the \mbox{\hyperlink{group__avoptions_gac14db824af52baf8181406e98d116097}{av\+\_\+opt\+\_\+free()}} function to automatically free all the allocated string and binary options.

Continuing with the above example\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}

\DoxyCodeLine{    \mbox{\hyperlink{group__avoptions_gad4ca968e9058b39b2da630ad0a091bdb}{av\_opt\_set\_defaults}}(\mbox{\hyperlink{filter__design_8txt_af1ec77bdca1b30e8153fc5da88f603db}{ret}});}

\hypertarget{group__avoptions_avoptions_implement_nesting}{}\doxysubsubsection{Nesting}\label{group__avoptions_avoptions_implement_nesting}
It may happen that an A\+V\+Options-\/enabled struct contains another A\+V\+Options-\/enabled struct as a member (e.\+g. \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_a_v_codec_context}{A\+V\+Codec\+Context}} in libavcodec exports generic options, while its priv\+\_\+data field exports codec-\/specific options). In such a case, it is possible to set up the parent struct to export a child\textquotesingle{}s options. To do that, simply implement \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_a_v_class_a1e996ee57c93f5513281c04f68440cff}{A\+V\+Class.\+child\+\_\+next()}} and \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_a_v_class_a6bb76293fc5966e135787d27bda06382}{A\+V\+Class.\+child\+\_\+class\+\_\+iterate()}} in the parent struct\textquotesingle{}s \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_a_v_class}{A\+V\+Class}}. Assuming that the test\+\_\+struct from above now also contains a child\+\_\+struct field\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keyword}{typedef} \textcolor{keyword}{struct }child\_struct \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{    \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_a_v_class}{AVClass}} *\textcolor{keyword}{class};}
\DoxyCodeLine{    \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} flags\_opt;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\} child\_struct;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_a_v_option}{AVOption}} child\_opts[] = \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{    \{ \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}test\_flags"{}}, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}This is a test option of flags type."{}},}
\DoxyCodeLine{      offsetof(child\_struct, flags\_opt), \mbox{\hyperlink{group__avoptions_ggabd75aa30eb8ad6387672df9a1fa79444a7aaeee142b88a3078ddc57c644b49a7e}{AV\_OPT\_TYPE\_FLAGS}}, \{ .i64 = 0 \}, INT\_MIN, INT\_MAX \},}
\DoxyCodeLine{    \{ \mbox{\hyperlink{coverity_8c_a070d2ce7b6bb7e5c05602aa8c308d0c4}{NULL}} \},}
\DoxyCodeLine{\};}

\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keywordtype}{void} *\mbox{\hyperlink{vf__spp_8c_a9f4f52ed63c57fc1247eae840c1bf735}{child\_next}}(\textcolor{keywordtype}{void} *obj, \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} *prev)}

\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_a_v_class}{AVClass}} \mbox{\hyperlink{vf__scale_8c_a4e01dac4b615d20e648f349fc670fcd7}{child\_class\_iterate}}(\textcolor{keywordtype}{void} **iter)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\{}
\DoxyCodeLine{    \textcolor{keyword}{const} \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_a_v_class}{AVClass}} *\mbox{\hyperlink{undefined_8txt_a12d8853991e25cc8d069554379c29ef6}{c}} = *iter ? \mbox{\hyperlink{coverity_8c_a070d2ce7b6bb7e5c05602aa8c308d0c4}{NULL}} : \&child\_class;}
\DoxyCodeLine{    *iter = (\textcolor{keywordtype}{void}*)(uintptr\_t)\mbox{\hyperlink{undefined_8txt_a12d8853991e25cc8d069554379c29ef6}{c}};}
\DoxyCodeLine{    \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} \mbox{\hyperlink{undefined_8txt_a12d8853991e25cc8d069554379c29ef6}{c}};}
\DoxyCodeLine{\}}
\end{DoxyCode}
 Putting \mbox{\hyperlink{vf__spp_8c_a9f4f52ed63c57fc1247eae840c1bf735}{child\+\_\+next()}} and \mbox{\hyperlink{vf__scale_8c_a4e01dac4b615d20e648f349fc670fcd7}{child\+\_\+class\+\_\+iterate()}} as defined above into test\+\_\+class will now make child\+\_\+struct\textquotesingle{}s options accessible through test\+\_\+struct (again, proper setup as described above needs to be done on child\+\_\+struct right after it is created).

From the above example it might not be clear why both \mbox{\hyperlink{vf__spp_8c_a9f4f52ed63c57fc1247eae840c1bf735}{child\+\_\+next()}} and \mbox{\hyperlink{vf__scale_8c_a4e01dac4b615d20e648f349fc670fcd7}{child\+\_\+class\+\_\+iterate()}} are needed. The distinction is that \mbox{\hyperlink{vf__spp_8c_a9f4f52ed63c57fc1247eae840c1bf735}{child\+\_\+next()}} iterates over actually existing objects, while \mbox{\hyperlink{vf__scale_8c_a4e01dac4b615d20e648f349fc670fcd7}{child\+\_\+class\+\_\+iterate()}} iterates over all possible child classes. E.\+g. if an \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_a_v_codec_context}{A\+V\+Codec\+Context}} was initialized to use a codec which has private options, then its \mbox{\hyperlink{vf__spp_8c_a9f4f52ed63c57fc1247eae840c1bf735}{child\+\_\+next()}} will return \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_a_v_codec_context_af3379123060ad8cc9c321c29af4f8360}{A\+V\+Codec\+Context.\+priv\+\_\+data}} and finish iterating. O\+T\+OH \mbox{\hyperlink{vf__scale_8c_a4e01dac4b615d20e648f349fc670fcd7}{child\+\_\+class\+\_\+iterate()}} on \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_a_v_codec_context_a90622d3af2a9abba986a1c9f7ca21b16}{A\+V\+Codec\+Context.\+av\+\_\+class}} will iterate over all available codecs with private options.\hypertarget{group__avoptions_avoptions_implement_named_constants}{}\doxysubsubsection{Named constants}\label{group__avoptions_avoptions_implement_named_constants}
It is possible to create named constants for options. Simply set the unit field of the option the constants should apply to a string and create the constants themselves as options of type A\+V\+\_\+\+O\+P\+T\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+P\+E\+\_\+\+C\+O\+N\+ST with their unit field set to the same string. Their default\+\_\+val field should contain the value of the named constant. For example, to add some named constants for the test\+\_\+flags option above, put the following into the child\+\_\+opts array\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\{ \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}test\_flags"{}}, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}This is a test option of flags type."{}},}
\DoxyCodeLine{  offsetof(child\_struct, flags\_opt), \mbox{\hyperlink{group__avoptions_ggabd75aa30eb8ad6387672df9a1fa79444a7aaeee142b88a3078ddc57c644b49a7e}{AV\_OPT\_TYPE\_FLAGS}}, \{ .i64 = 0 \}, INT\_MIN, INT\_MAX, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}test\_unit"{}} \},}
\DoxyCodeLine{\{ \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}flag1"{}}, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}This is a flag with value 16"{}}, 0, \mbox{\hyperlink{group__avoptions_ggabd75aa30eb8ad6387672df9a1fa79444a0fa9f07d428bdc32495fe55c365c5329}{AV\_OPT\_TYPE\_CONST}}, \{ .i64 = 16 \}, 0, 0, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}test\_unit"{}} \},}
\end{DoxyCode}
\hypertarget{group__avoptions_avoptions_use}{}\doxysubsection{Using A\+V\+Options}\label{group__avoptions_avoptions_use}
This section deals with accessing options in an A\+V\+Options-\/enabled struct. Such structs in F\+Fmpeg are e.\+g. \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_a_v_codec_context}{A\+V\+Codec\+Context}} in libavcodec or \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_a_v_format_context}{A\+V\+Format\+Context}} in libavformat.\hypertarget{group__avoptions_avoptions_use_examine}{}\doxysubsubsection{Examining A\+V\+Options}\label{group__avoptions_avoptions_use_examine}
The basic functions for examining options are \mbox{\hyperlink{group__avoptions_gabc75970cd87d1bf47a4ff449470e9225}{av\+\_\+opt\+\_\+next()}}, which iterates over all options defined for one object, and \mbox{\hyperlink{group__avoptions_gae31ae7fb20113b00108d0ecf53f25664}{av\+\_\+opt\+\_\+find()}}, which searches for an option with the given name.

The situation is more complicated with nesting. An A\+V\+Options-\/enabled struct may have A\+V\+Options-\/enabled children. Passing the A\+V\+\_\+\+O\+P\+T\+\_\+\+S\+E\+A\+R\+C\+H\+\_\+\+C\+H\+I\+L\+D\+R\+EN flag to \mbox{\hyperlink{group__avoptions_gae31ae7fb20113b00108d0ecf53f25664}{av\+\_\+opt\+\_\+find()}} will make the function search children recursively.

For enumerating there are basically two cases. The first is when you want to get all options that may potentially exist on the struct and its children (e.\+g. when constructing documentation). In that case you should call \mbox{\hyperlink{group__avoptions_gaecaeff32911c84f16ca9378630c33692}{av\+\_\+opt\+\_\+child\+\_\+class\+\_\+iterate()}} recursively on the parent struct\textquotesingle{}s \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_a_v_class}{A\+V\+Class}}. The second case is when you have an already initialized struct with all its children and you want to get all options that can be actually written or read from it. In that case you should call \mbox{\hyperlink{group__avoptions_gaacce30022d2e99c7b9309d3ad3345f69}{av\+\_\+opt\+\_\+child\+\_\+next()}} recursively (and \mbox{\hyperlink{group__avoptions_gabc75970cd87d1bf47a4ff449470e9225}{av\+\_\+opt\+\_\+next()}} on each result).\hypertarget{group__avoptions_avoptions_use_get_set}{}\doxysubsubsection{Reading and writing A\+V\+Options}\label{group__avoptions_avoptions_use_get_set}
When setting options, you often have a string read directly from the user. In such a case, simply passing it to \mbox{\hyperlink{group__opt__set__funcs_ga5fd4b92bdf4f392a2847f711676a7537}{av\+\_\+opt\+\_\+set()}} is enough. For non-\/string type options, \mbox{\hyperlink{group__opt__set__funcs_ga5fd4b92bdf4f392a2847f711676a7537}{av\+\_\+opt\+\_\+set()}} will parse the string according to the option type.

Similarly \mbox{\hyperlink{group__opt__get__funcs_gaf31144e60f9ce89dbe8cbea57a0b232c}{av\+\_\+opt\+\_\+get()}} will read any option type and convert it to a string which will be returned. Do not forget that the string is allocated, so you have to free it with \mbox{\hyperlink{tableprint__vlc_8h_a079eab092887563f2bef9106c6120089}{av\+\_\+free()}}.

In some cases it may be more convenient to put all options into an \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_a_v_dictionary}{A\+V\+Dictionary}} and call \mbox{\hyperlink{group__avoptions_gaf1a88e8f152d7835f111b1ef8813fb2e}{av\+\_\+opt\+\_\+set\+\_\+dict()}} on it. A specific case of this are the format/codec open functions in lavf/lavc which take a dictionary filled with option as a parameter. This makes it possible to set some options that cannot be set otherwise, since e.\+g. the input file format is not known before the file is actually opened.

When selecting this format for a decoder, \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_a_v_codec_context_a3bac44bb0b016ab838780cc19ac277d6}{A\+V\+Codec\+Context.\+hw\+\_\+frames\+\_\+ctx}} should be set to a suitable frames context inside the \mbox{\hyperlink{doc_2examples_2qsvdec_8c_afe1023087c26d2d410c9cd7d491c8660}{get\+\_\+format()}} callback. The frames context must have been created on a device of the specified type.

When selecting this format for an encoder, \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_a_v_codec_context_a3bac44bb0b016ab838780cc19ac277d6}{A\+V\+Codec\+Context.\+hw\+\_\+frames\+\_\+ctx}} should be set to the context which will be used for the input frames before calling \mbox{\hyperlink{group__lavc__core_ga11f785a188d7d9df71621001465b0f1d}{avcodec\+\_\+open2()}}. \\

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{ffmpeg__filter_8c_a61569f2965b7a369eb10b6d75d410d11}{int}} av\+\_\+opt\+\_\+copy (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{rematrix__template_8c_a4dfdfbb7b69470f1152e022432ee2d45}{void}} $\ast$}]{dest,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{rematrix__template_8c_a4dfdfbb7b69470f1152e022432ee2d45}{void}} $\ast$}]{src }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Copy options from src object into dest object.

Options that require memory allocation (e.\+g. string or binary) are malloc\textquotesingle{}ed in dest object. Original memory allocated for such options is freed unless both src and dest options points to the same memory.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em dest} & Object to copy from \\
\hline
{\em src} & Object to copy into \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 on success, negative on error 
\end{DoxyReturn}

Look for an option in an object. Consider only options which have all the specified flags set.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em obj} & A pointer to a struct whose first element is a pointer to an \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_a_v_class}{A\+V\+Class}}. Alternatively a double pointer to an \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_a_v_class}{A\+V\+Class}}, if A\+V\+\_\+\+O\+P\+T\+\_\+\+S\+E\+A\+R\+C\+H\+\_\+\+F\+A\+K\+E\+\_\+\+O\+BJ search flag is set. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em name} & The name of the option to look for. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em unit} & When searching for named constants, name of the unit it belongs to. \\
\hline
 & {\em opt\+\_\+flags} & Find only options with all the specified flags set (A\+V\+\_\+\+O\+P\+T\+\_\+\+F\+L\+AG). \\
\hline
 & {\em search\+\_\+flags} & A combination of A\+V\+\_\+\+O\+P\+T\+\_\+\+S\+E\+A\+R\+C\+H\+\_\+$\ast$.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
A pointer to the option found, or N\+U\+LL if no option was found.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Options found with A\+V\+\_\+\+O\+P\+T\+\_\+\+S\+E\+A\+R\+C\+H\+\_\+\+C\+H\+I\+L\+D\+R\+EN flag may not be settable directly with \mbox{\hyperlink{group__opt__set__funcs_ga5fd4b92bdf4f392a2847f711676a7537}{av\+\_\+opt\+\_\+set()}}. Use special calls which take an options \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_a_v_dictionary}{A\+V\+Dictionary}} (e.\+g. \mbox{\hyperlink{group__lavf__decoding_gaff468dcc45289542f4c30d311bc2a201}{avformat\+\_\+open\+\_\+input()}}) to set options found with this flag. 
\end{DoxyNote}

Check if given option is set to its default value.

Options o must belong to the obj. This function must not be called to check child\textquotesingle{}s options state. \begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\mbox{\hyperlink{group__avoptions_gaa37a02c9d3e6d9f049f2e7174811f5fb}{av\+\_\+opt\+\_\+is\+\_\+set\+\_\+to\+\_\+default\+\_\+by\+\_\+name()}}.
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\index{av\_opt\_serialize@{av\_opt\_serialize}!AVOptions@{AVOptions}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{av\_opt\_serialize()}{av\_opt\_serialize()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{ffmpeg__filter_8c_a61569f2965b7a369eb10b6d75d410d11}{int}} av\+\_\+opt\+\_\+serialize (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{rematrix__template_8c_a4dfdfbb7b69470f1152e022432ee2d45}{void}} $\ast$}]{obj,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{ffmpeg__filter_8c_a61569f2965b7a369eb10b6d75d410d11}{int}}}]{opt\+\_\+flags,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{ffmpeg__filter_8c_a61569f2965b7a369eb10b6d75d410d11}{int}}}]{flags,  }\item[{char $\ast$$\ast$}]{buffer,  }\item[{const char}]{key\+\_\+val\+\_\+sep,  }\item[{const char}]{pairs\+\_\+sep }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Serialize object\textquotesingle{}s options.

Create a string containing object\textquotesingle{}s serialized options. Such string may be passed back to \mbox{\hyperlink{group__avoptions_gaa936b1aa7caca67b21cd50819c2b9fb1}{av\+\_\+opt\+\_\+set\+\_\+from\+\_\+string()}} in order to restore option values. A key/value or pairs separator occurring in the serialized value or name string are escaped through the \mbox{\hyperlink{group__lavu__string_ga3c5e00d3f0575f2a3858f837656c08e9}{av\+\_\+escape()}} function.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em obj} & \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_a_v_class}{A\+V\+Class}} object to serialize \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em opt\+\_\+flags} & serialize options with all the specified flags set (A\+V\+\_\+\+O\+P\+T\+\_\+\+F\+L\+AG) \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em flags} & combination of A\+V\+\_\+\+O\+P\+T\+\_\+\+S\+E\+R\+I\+A\+L\+I\+Z\+E\+\_\+$\ast$ flags \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em buffer} & Pointer to buffer that will be allocated with string containg serialized options. Buffer must be freed by the caller when is no longer needed. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em key\+\_\+val\+\_\+sep} & character used to separate key from value \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ in}}  & {\em pairs\+\_\+sep} & character used to separate two pairs from each other \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
$>$= 0 on success, negative on error 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyWarning}{Warning}
Separators cannot be neither \textquotesingle{}\textbackslash{}\textquotesingle{} nor \textquotesingle{}\textbackslash{}0\textquotesingle{}. They also cannot be the same. 
\end{DoxyWarning}

Set all the options from a given dictionary on an object.

\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em obj} & a struct whose first element is a pointer to \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_a_v_class}{A\+V\+Class}} \\
\hline
{\em options} & options to process. This dictionary will be freed and replaced by a new one containing all options not found in obj. Of course this new dictionary needs to be freed by caller with \mbox{\hyperlink{group__lavu__dict_ga1bafd682b1fbb90e48a4cc3814b820f7}{av\+\_\+dict\+\_\+free()}}. \\
\hline
{\em search\+\_\+flags} & A combination of A\+V\+\_\+\+O\+P\+T\+\_\+\+S\+E\+A\+R\+C\+H\+\_\+$\ast$.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 on success, a negative A\+V\+E\+R\+R\+OR if some option was found in obj, but could not be set.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\mbox{\hyperlink{group__lavu__dict_ga59a6372b124b306e3a2233723c5cdc78}{av\+\_\+dict\+\_\+copy()}} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{av\_opt\_set\_from\_string()}{av\_opt\_set\_from\_string()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{ffmpeg__filter_8c_a61569f2965b7a369eb10b6d75d410d11}{int}} av\+\_\+opt\+\_\+set\+\_\+from\+\_\+string (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{rematrix__template_8c_a4dfdfbb7b69470f1152e022432ee2d45}{void}} $\ast$}]{ctx,  }\item[{const char $\ast$}]{opts,  }\item[{const char $\ast$const $\ast$}]{shorthand,  }\item[{const char $\ast$}]{key\+\_\+val\+\_\+sep,  }\item[{const char $\ast$}]{pairs\+\_\+sep }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Parse the key-\/value pairs list in opts. For each key=value pair found, set the value of the corresponding option in ctx.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em ctx} & the \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_a_v_class}{A\+V\+Class}} object to set options on \\
\hline
{\em opts} & the options string, key-\/value pairs separated by a delimiter \\
\hline
{\em shorthand} & a N\+U\+L\+L-\/terminated array of options names for shorthand notation\+: if the first field in opts has no key part, the key is taken from the first element of shorthand; then again for the second, etc., until either opts is finished, shorthand is finished or a named option is found; after that, all options must be named \\
\hline
{\em key\+\_\+val\+\_\+sep} & a 0-\/terminated list of characters used to separate key from value, for example \textquotesingle{}=\textquotesingle{} \\
\hline
{\em pairs\+\_\+sep} & a 0-\/terminated list of characters used to separate two pairs from each other, for example \textquotesingle{}\+:\textquotesingle{} or \textquotesingle{},\textquotesingle{} \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
the number of successfully set key=value pairs, or a negative value corresponding to an A\+V\+E\+R\+R\+OR code in case of error\+: \mbox{\hyperlink{group__lavu__error_gae4bb6f165973d09584e0ec0f335f69ca}{A\+V\+E\+R\+R\+O\+R(\+E\+I\+N\+V\+A\+L)}} if opts cannot be parsed, the error code issued by av\+\_\+set\+\_\+string3() if a key/value pair cannot be set
\end{DoxyReturn}
Options names must use only the following characters\+: a-\/z A-\/Z 0-\/9 -\/ . / \+\_\+ Separators must use characters distinct from option names and from each other.

\index{AVOptions@{AVOptions}!av\_set\_options\_string@{av\_set\_options\_string}}
\index{av\_set\_options\_string@{av\_set\_options\_string}!AVOptions@{AVOptions}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{av\_set\_options\_string()}{av\_set\_options\_string()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{ffmpeg__filter_8c_a61569f2965b7a369eb10b6d75d410d11}{int}} av\+\_\+set\+\_\+options\+\_\+string (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{rematrix__template_8c_a4dfdfbb7b69470f1152e022432ee2d45}{void}} $\ast$}]{ctx,  }\item[{const char $\ast$}]{opts,  }\item[{const char $\ast$}]{key\+\_\+val\+\_\+sep,  }\item[{const char $\ast$}]{pairs\+\_\+sep }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Parse the key/value pairs list in opts. For each key/value pair found, stores the value in the field in ctx that is named like the key. ctx must be an \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_a_v_class}{A\+V\+Class}} context, storing is done using A\+V\+Options.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em opts} & options string to parse, may be N\+U\+LL \\
\hline
{\em key\+\_\+val\+\_\+sep} & a 0-\/terminated list of characters used to separate key from value \\
\hline
{\em pairs\+\_\+sep} & a 0-\/terminated list of characters used to separate two pairs from each other \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
the number of successfully set key/value pairs, or a negative value corresponding to an A\+V\+E\+R\+R\+OR code in case of error\+: \mbox{\hyperlink{group__lavu__error_gae4bb6f165973d09584e0ec0f335f69ca}{A\+V\+E\+R\+R\+O\+R(\+E\+I\+N\+V\+A\+L)}} if opts cannot be parsed, the error code issued by \mbox{\hyperlink{group__opt__set__funcs_ga5fd4b92bdf4f392a2847f711676a7537}{av\+\_\+opt\+\_\+set()}} if a key/value pair cannot be set 
\end{DoxyReturn}
